> bool libHMDV_gt_HeroMedivhForceofWillRemoveEarly_Func (bool testConds, bool runActions) {
>     // Automatic Variable Declarations
>     // Actions
>     if (!runActions) {
>         return true;
>     }
> 
>     while ((UnitBehaviorDuration(EventUnit(), "MedivhForceOfWill") > 0.0625)) {

>     return true;
